20159 = {
	name="Brandon"	
	dynasty=59
	
	martial=7
	diplomacy=10
	intrigue=5
	stewardship=6

	religion="old_gods"
	culture="northman"

	father=20059
	mother=40059
	
	add_trait=proud #Torhenn's sons were unhappy with his kneeling
	add_trait=ambitious

	7975.1.1 = {birth="7975.1.1"  }
	7991.1.1 = { add_trait=skilled_warrior }
	8014.1.1 = { add_trait="ice" }
	8025.1.1 = {add_spouse=40159}
	8043.1.1 = { #Faith Militant Uprising
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { year = 8044 } }
			}
			any_vassal = { 
				set_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = against_king
			}
			set_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = against_king
		}
	}
	8044.1.1 = { #Faith Militant Uprising
		effect = {
			any_vassal = { clr_character_flag = neutral  }
			clr_character_flag = neutral
		}
	}
	8047.12.12 = {death="8047.12.12"}
}

			}
		}
